country_event = {
	id = iran_md.1 # Flag change (alt hist)
	title = iran_md.1.t
	desc = iran_md.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_civil_war
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = iran_md.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:iran_md.1.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					PER = {
						nationalist_monarchists_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
				PER = { set_cosmetic_tag = PER_AUTH_PAN }
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = divide_turkey.2 # Iran Wants Us To Embargo Turkey for armenia
	title = divide_turkey.2.t
	desc = divide_turkey.2.d
	picture = GFX_TUR_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o1 executed"
		SOV = {
			send_embargo = TUR
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = divide_turkey.2.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:divide_turkey.2.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		PER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = SOV
				modifier = small_decrease
			}
		}
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = divide_turkey.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = development_plan.1 # The Third Development Plan
	title = development_plan.1.t
	desc = development_plan.1.d
	picture = GFX_iran_majles
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Industry
		name = development_plan.1.o1
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o1 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = industry_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_industry
	}
	option = { # Science
		name = development_plan.1.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o2 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = science_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_science
	}
	option = { # Military
		name = development_plan.1.o3
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:development_plan.1.o3 executed"
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = military_focus_idea
			days = 1825
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_development_plan_option_military
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = reorganize_school.1
	title = reorganize_school.t
	desc = reorganize_school.d
	picture = GFX_school_reorganize
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.a
		log = "l"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_2
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_3
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = reorganize_school.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 2
		}
		swap_ideas = {
		remove_idea = PER_reorganize_school_1
		add_idea = PER_reorganize_school_4
		}
	}
}

	title = PER_contact_k.2.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.2.desc
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #offer money
		name = PER_contact_k.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_k.2.a executed"

			base = 4
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {

			}
		}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.6 # Deal goes through
	title = PER_contact_k.6.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.6.d
	picture = GFX_KOR_nuke_deal
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #accept tech
		name = PER_contact_k.6.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_tech_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				add_tech_bonus = {
					bonus = 0.15
					uses = 2
					category = CAT_industry
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_resource_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				create_import = {
					resource = oil
					amount = 16
					exporter = PER
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_moni_KOR
				}
			}
			KOR = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			PER = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_contact_k.7 # Iran goes to NK
	title = PER_contact_k.7.t
	desc = PER_contact_k.7.d
	picture = GFX_hung_2020
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #contact NK
		name = PER_contact_k.7.a
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			KOR = {
				has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
				has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
			}
			country_exists = NKO
		}
		NKO = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_contact_nk.1
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #No one else
		name = PER_contact_k.7.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 7
		}
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				KOR = {
					has_country_flag = PER_no_moni_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_resource_KOR
					has_country_flag = PER_no_tech_KOR
				}
				NOT = {
					country_exists = NKO
				}
			}
		}
		KOR = {
			set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_1
		}
	}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_k.7.c
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
		set_country_flag = PER_KOR_nd_2
	}
}

				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_tech_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					add_tech_bonus = {
						bonus = 0.15
						uses = 2
						category = CAT_industry
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_resource_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					create_import = {
						resource = oil
						amount = 16
						exporter = PER
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NKO = {
						has_country_flag = PER_moni_NKO
					}
				}
				NKO = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
				PER = {
					set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
					modify_treasury_effect = yes
				}
			}
		}
	option = { #decline
		name = PER_contact_nk.6.b
		log = null
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
		PER = {
			set_country_flag = PER_NKO_nd_2
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

			base = 25
		}
		add_popularity = { # Increase Emerging
			ideology = communism
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }

		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		random_list = {
			40 = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ruling_party = communism
					ideology = neutrality
					size = 0.2
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					remove_opinion_modifier = {
						target = PER
						modifier = no_diplomatic_ties

							target = TUR

					}

						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					ARM = {
						break_embargo = TUR
					}
					TUR = {
						NATO_leave = yes
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } } }
							hidden_effect = {
								clear_array = ruling_party
								clear_array = gov_coalition_array
								add_to_array = { ruling_party = 6 }
								update_government_coalition_strength = yes
								update_party_name = yes
								set_coalition_drift = yes
								set_ruling_leader = yes
								set_leader = yes
							}
							set_politics = {
								ruling_party = communism
								elections_allowed = no
							}
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}
						else_if = {
							limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
							set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
							set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
							set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
							add_relative_party_popularity = yes
						}

						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = GER }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes

						set_temp_variable = { percent_change = -100 }
						set_temp_variable = { tag_index = ENG }
						set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
						change_influence_percentage = yes
					}
				}
			}
			60 = {
				hidden_effect = {
					NATO_leave = yes
					set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
					set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 1.00 }
					add_relative_party_popularity = yes
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					if = {

							clear_array = ruling_party

							set_leader = yes

							ruling_party = communism
							elections_allowed = no
						}

						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }
						set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = 0.05 }
						add_relative_party_popularity = yes
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { is_in_array = { ruling_party = 6 } }
						set_temp_variable = { party_index = 6 }
						set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.15 }

			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_half_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_one_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_one_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_one_billion_weekly
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { PER = { has_country_flag = PER_ask_iraq_for_two_billion_weekly } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_two_billion_weekly_money_TT
			PER = { set_country_flag = PER_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly }
			set_country_flag = IRQ_iraq_accepted_to_pay_two_billion_weekly
		}
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.54 } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_contact_with_countries.52.o2 executed"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = PER_iran_attack_iraq_wargoal_TT
		hidden_effect = { PER = { country_event = { id = PER_contact_with_countries.53 } } }
	}
}

country_event = { #Turkey accepts
	id = PER_orupa.2
	title = PER_orupa.2.t
	desc = PER_orupa.2.d
	picture = GFX_orupa

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
	name = PER_orupa.2.a
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_orupa.2.a executed"
	set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -0.16 }
	modify_treasury_effect = yes
		build_railway = {
		  level = 1
		  path = { 9893 3899 11746 11810 9830 9763 9755 940 11860 9878 3983 3951 3786 11811 11829 9833 }
		  start_province = 9893
		  target_province = 9833
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				add_ideas = { PER_TUR_shia_influence }
				set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 2 }
				set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
				set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
				change_influence_percentage = yes
				add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_index = 9 }
				set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = 0.10 }
				add_relative_party_popularity = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = democratic
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = democratic popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = nationalist
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = nationalist popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = neutrality popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = fascism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = communism
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
						emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 5 }
			set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
			set_temp_variable = { influence_target = TUR }
			change_influence_percentage = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = communism popularity = 0.05 }
		}
		GRE = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		BUL = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_orupa.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
	name = PER_orupa.2.b
	log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_orupa.2.b executed"
	}
}

					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1

					level = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}

			limit = {

						GER = { has_country_flag = GER_mediation_support }

### Iranian Presidental Elections Events ###

country_event = { # Event to automatically choose presidents based on popularity and date
	id = PER_election_events.1
	title = PER_election_events.1.t
	desc = PER_election_events.1.d
	picture = GFX_election
	trigger = {
		tag = PER
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		}
		OR = {
			date > 2001.2.1
			date > 2005.2.1
			date > 2009.2.1
			date > 2013.2.1
			date > 2017.2.1
			date > 2021.2.1
		}

	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	timeout_days = 1
	immediate = {
		if = { #8th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2001.1.1
				date < 2002.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.2
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #9th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2005.1.1
				date < 2006.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.3
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #10th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2009.1.1
				date < 2010.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.4
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #11th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2013.1.1
				date < 2014.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.5
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #12th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2017.1.1
				date < 2018.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.6
				days = 0
			}
		}
		else_if = { #13th Period
			limit = {
				date > 2021.1.1
				date < 2022.1.1
			}
			country_event = {
				id = PER_election_events.7
				days = 0
			}
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.1.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.1.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}
}

country_event = { # 2001 Election Notification (Between Khatami and Tavakkoli)
	id = PER_election_events.2
	title = PER_election_events.2.t
	desc = PER_election_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_election
	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		has_government = communism
		OR = {
			emerging_hardline_shiite_are_in_power = yes
			emerging_moderate_shiite_are_in_power = yes
		}
		tag = PER
		date > 2001.3.1
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = PER_fix_shit
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	timeout_days = 30
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ahmadinejad
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_raisi
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_tavakoli
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_ghalibaf
		clr_country_flag = principalist_portrait_rezaee
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_hemmati
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_khatami
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_mousavi
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rafsanjani
		clr_country_flag = reformist_portrait_rouhani

		set_country_flag = PER_election_enabled
		set_country_flag = principalist_portrait_tavakoli
		set_country_flag = reformist_portrait_khatami
		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = PER_auto_update_gui_weekly
		}
	}


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.2.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.2.a executed"
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = PER_Iranian_elections_decision_category
	}

country_event = { # Khatami Elected as President 2001 (Reformists Won)
	id = PER_election_events.8
	title = PER_election_events.8.t
	desc = PER_election_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_khatami_won_election
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = PER_election_events.8.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_election_events.8.a executed"

		PER_scripted_effect_update_principalists_popularity_variable = yes

		set_temp_variable = { rul_party_temp = 8 }
		change_ruling_party_effect = yes

		PER_scripted_effect_finish_election = yes
		set_country_flag = PER_president_khatami # Set President
		add_to_variable = { iranian_president_change = 1 }
		add_ideas = PER_khatami_idea
	}
}

country_event = { #Meant for player
	id = PER_revolution.15
	title = PER_revolution.15.t
	desc = PER_revolution.15.d
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_mek_rebellion
	option = { #This is it for them!
		name = PER_revolution.15.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_revolution.15.a executed"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = do_not_retire

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
					is_in_array = { ruling_party = 0 } #Pahlavi
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = communism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 7 } #Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 4 } #Communist-State
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 8 } #Moderate Shiite
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 9 } #Hardline Shiite
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = communism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = fascism
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 11 } #Caliphate
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 10 } #Kingdom
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = neutrality
					OR = {
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 13 } #Neutral_Autocracy
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 18 } #neutral socialist
						is_in_array = { ruling_party = 19 } #neutral communist
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = nationalist

			50 = {

			}

		}

country_event = { #Iran offers help (IRQ)
	id = PER_political.20
	title = PER_political.20.t
	desc = PER_political.20.d
	picture = GFX_handshake_black
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ok
		name = PER_political.20.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.20.a executed"
		set_country_flag = irq_says_yes_aid
		set_temp_variable = { percent_change = 1 }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_index = PER }
		set_temp_variable = { influence_target = IRQ }
		change_influence_percentage = yes
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_political.201
				days = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = irq_says_yes_aid
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
	option = { #No
		name = PER_political.20.b
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.20.b executed"
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_political.202
				days = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = irq_says_no_aid
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Cuba Accepts
	id = PER_political.211
	title = PER_political.211.t
	desc = PER_political.211.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Okay
		name = PER_political.211.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.211.a executed"
		CUB = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = PER
				modifier = military_cooperation
			}
			give_military_access = PER
		}
		PER = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CUB
				modifier = military_cooperation
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
	}
}

		AFG = {

			}
		}
		AFG = { every_core_state = { add_core_of = PER } }
		hidden_effect = {
			PER = {
				country_event = {
					id = PER_political.87878
					days = 0
				}
			}
			414 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			412 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			415 = {
				transfer_state_to = TAL
			}
			TAL = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PER
					type = puppet_wargoal_focus
				}
			}
			TAL = {
				division_template = {
					name = "Taliban"
					regiments = {
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 1 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 2 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 3 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 1 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 2 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 3 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 2 y = 0 }
						Special_Forces = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					}
					priority = 2
				}
				capital_scope = {
					create_unit = {
						division = "name = \"Taliban\" division_template = \"Taliban\" start_experience_factor = 1.0"
						owner = TAL
						count = 15
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 6
		}
	}

			create_wargoal = {
				type = annex_everything
				target = AFG
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 4
		}
	}
}

	id = PER_political.9865
	title = PER_political.9865.t
	desc = PER_political.9865.d

		name = PER_political.9865.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.9865.a executed"
		PER = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_political.98651
				days = 1
			}
		}
		#
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "No Step Back" }
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 35.29 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			PER = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -35.29 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			PER = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = mbt_hull_1
					variant_name = "Leopard 2A5"
					amount = 100
					producer = GER
				}
			}
			GER = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = mbt_hull_1
					variant_name = "Leopard 2A5"
					amount = -100
					producer = GER
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = 35.29 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
			PER = {
				set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -35.29 }
				modify_treasury_effect = yes
			}
			PER = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = MBT_1
					amount = 100
					producer = GER
				}
			}
			GER = {
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = MBT_1
					amount = -100
					producer = GER
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				has_opinion = { target = PER value > 20 }
				add = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # No

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_political.9865.b executed"

	}

country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.3
	title = PER_civilwar.3.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_civil_war_event_4
	option = { # Those bastards
		name = PER_civilwar.3.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.3.a executed"
		news_event = {
			id = PER_rev_flavor.1
			days = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = large_plane_air_transport_airframe_1
				variant_name = "C-130 Hercules"
				amount = -1
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = transport_plane1
				amount = -1
				producer = USA
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = PER_civilwar.4
				days = 3
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = PER_civilwar.104
	title = PER_civilwar.104.t
	desc = PER_civilwar.104.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	# Removes units
	option = {
		name = PER_civilwar.104.a
		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]:PER_civilwar.104.a executed"
		ZOR = {
			add_ideas = international_bankers
			add_ideas = farmers
			add_ideas = landowners
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = PER
				}
				declare_war_on = { target = ROOT type = civil_war }
				ROOT = {
					every_core_state = {
						remove_core_of = ZOR
						set_state_flag = ZOR_core_4_later  #this dont work womp womp
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = PER_Zoroastrian_spawned
			add_ideas = PER_Zoroastrianism_Flame_of_Resistance
			add_state_core = 977
			add_state_core = 1147
			PER = { declare_war_on = { target = ZOR type = civil_war } }
			declare_war_on = { target = IRI type = civil_war }
			MOJ = { create_wargoal = { target = ZOR type = civil_war } }
			1147 = { transfer_state_to = HRM }
			transfer_units_fraction = {
				target = HRM
				size = 1.0
				stockpile_ratio = 0
				army_ratio = 1.0
				navy_ratio = 0
				air_ratio = 0
			}
			1147 = { transfer_state_to = ZOR }
			set_province_controller = 14673
			1147 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no }
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ISI
				}
				IRI = { set_state_controller = 1147 }
				else = {
					PER = { set_state_controller = 1147 }
				}
			}
			set_province_controller = 14673
			PER = { set_province_controller = 14263 }
			division_template = {
				name = "Lashkar-e Yazd" #dont know what to call this
				regiments = {
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					Special_Forces = { x = 0 y = 3 }
					Special_Forces = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					SP_Arty_Bat = { x = 1 y = 1 }
				}
				support = {
					L_Engi_Comp = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					SP_AA_Battery = { x = 0 y = 1 }
				}
			}
			1147 = { create_unit = { division = "name = \"Lashkar-e Rostam\" division_template = \"Lashkar-e Motorizeh\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" owner = ROOT count = 1 } }
			1147 = { create_unit = { division = "name = \"Lashkar-e Zāl\" division_template = \"Lashkar-e Motorizeh\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" owner = ROOT count = 1 } }
			1147 = { create_unit = { division = "name = \"Lashkar-e Esfandiyār\" division_template = \"Lashkar-e Motorizeh\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" owner = ROOT count = 1 } }
			1147 = { create_unit = { division = "name = \"Lashkar-e Lohrasp\" division_template = \"Lashkar-e Motorizeh\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" owner = ROOT count = 1 } }
			1147 = { create_unit = { division = "name = \"Lashkar-e Mehrāb\" division_template = \"Lashkar-e Motorizeh\" start_experience_factor = 1.0" owner = ROOT count = 1 } }
			#Licence produced German G3 rifle
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_weapons amount = 14000 producer = GER }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = Anti_Air_1 amount = 20 producer = USA }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = Anti_Air_0 amount = 22 producer = SOV }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_0 amount = 2 producer = CHI }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = command_control_equipment1 amount = 34 }
			#i need to find out how to get rid of the civil war units
			#delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "IRGC Marine Brigade" disband = yes }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = PER
			}
			declare_war_on = { target = ZOR type = annex_everything }
		}
		#no news events
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

						check_variable = { influence_array^3 = USA }
						check_variable = { influence_array^4 = USA }
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_8
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_fighting_foreigners
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_9
					has_equipment = {
						Kamikaze_drone_equipment > 4999
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_the_supplier_of_martyrs
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_10
					408 = {
						agriculture_district > 0
					}
					408 = {
						agriculture_district > 0
					}
					408 = {
						agriculture_district > 0
					}
					408 = {
						agriculture_district > 0
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_aiding_the_farmer
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_11
					1146 = {
						infrastructure > 4
						fuel_silo > 4
					}
					399 = {
						infrastructure > 4
						fuel_silo > 4
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_fueling_our_revolution
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_12
					has_army_manpower = {
						size > 449999
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_outnumbering_the_enemy
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_13
					has_stability > 74
					OR = {
						has_idea = police_04
						has_idea = police_05
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_safety_with_stability
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_14
					403 = {
						missile_silo > 4
					}
					399 = {
						missile_silo > 4
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_national_deterrents
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_15
					OR = {
						IRQ = { has_idea = tribute_idea_PER	}
						SYR = { has_idea = tribute_idea_PER	}
						LEB = { has_idea = tribute_idea_PER	}
					}
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_exploiting_our_proxies
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = PER_did_principalists_16
					check_variable = { overall_productivity > 899.99 }
				}
			}
			activate_mission = PER_exploiting_our_proxies
		}

		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = PER_no_more_missions_TT
			set_country_flag = PER_principalists_clear
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}

		log = "[GetDateText]: [This.GetName]: PER_majlis.33.b executed"
		set_country_flag = {
			flag = PER_edu_cool_down_2
			days = 14
			value = 1
		}
		set_party_index_to_ruling_party = yes
		set_temp_variable = { party_popularity_increase = -0.015 }
		set_temp_variable = { temp_outlook_increase = -0.01 }
		add_relative_party_popularity = yes
		newline = yes
		add_political_power = -75
		newline = yes
		random_list = {
			20 = {
				block_social_change = yes
			}
			20 = {
				block_bureau_change = yes
			}
			60 = {}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
	}
}
